## TOPIC 01001: Counter Input:Pulse:Time:Input:Logic Level Behavior

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30b4.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30b4.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the logic level behavior on the count reset line. Remarks The following table lists the characteristics of this property. Short Name CI.Pulse.Time.LogicLvlBehavior Data type ci32.png Permissions Read/Write Resettable True Settable While Task Is Running device-specific Available in Run-Time

### Counter Input:Pulse:Time:Input:Logic Level Behavior

Specifies the logic level behavior on the count reset line.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.Pulse.Time.LogicLvlBehavior |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

| Logic Level Pull-up | 16064 | High logic. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| None | 10230 | Supply no excitation to the channel. |

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the digital threshold value in Volts for high and low input transitions. Some devices do not support this for differential channels. Remarks The following table lists the characteristics of this property. Short Name CI.ThreshVoltage Data type cdbl.png Permissions Read/Write Resettable True

### Counter Input:General Properties:Input Configuration:Voltage Threshold Level

Specifies the digital threshold value in Volts for high and low input transitions. Some devices do not support this for differential channels.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.ThreshVoltage |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

## TOPIC 01005: Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Advanced:Idle Output Behavior

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30b8.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30b8.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether this channel will disable excitation after the task is uncommitted. Setting this to Zero Volts or Amps disables excitation after task uncommit. Setting this attribute to Maintain Existing Value leaves the excitation on after task uncommit. Remarks The following table lists the char

### Analog Input:General Properties:Signal Conditioning:Excitation:Advanced:Idle Output Behavior

Specifies whether this channel will disable excitation after the task is uncommitted. Setting this to Zero Volts or Amps disables excitation after task uncommit. Setting this attribute to Maintain Existing Value leaves the excitation on after task uncommit.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | AI.Excit.IdleOutputBehavior |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

| Zero Volts or Amps | 12526 | Drive excitation output to zero. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Maintain Existing Value | 12528 | Continue generating the current value. |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

## TOPIC 01022: Counter Input:Velocity:Decoding Type

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30dc.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr30dc.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies how to count and interpret the pulses the encoder generates on signal A and signal B. X1, X2, and X4 are valid for quadrature encoders only. Two Pulse Counting is valid for two-pulse encoders only. Remarks The following table lists the characteristics of this property. Short Name CI.Veloci

### Counter Input:Velocity:Decoding Type

Specifies how to count and interpret the pulses the encoder generates on signal A and signal B. X1, X2, and X4 are valid for quadrature encoders only. Two Pulse Counting is valid for two-pulse encoders only.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.Velocity.Encoder.DecodingType |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

| X1 | 10090 | If signal A leads signal B, count the rising edges of signal A. If signal B leads signal A, count the falling edges of signal A. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| X2 | 10091 | Count the rising and falling edges of signal A. |
| X4 | 10092 | Count the rising and falling edges of signal A and signal B. |
| Two Pulse Counting | 10313 | Increment the count on rising edges of signal A. Decrement the count on rising edges of signal B. |

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 01065: Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Input Limits Fault Detection:Upper Limit

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr318c.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr318c.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the level of the upper limit for input limits detection. An input sample outside the upper and lower bounds causes a fault. Note: Fault detection applies to both positive and negative inputs. For instance, if you specify a lower limit of 2 mA and an upper limit of 12 mA, NI-DAQmx detects a

### Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Input Limits Fault Detection:Upper Limit

Specifies the level of the upper limit for input limits detection. An input sample outside the upper and lower bounds causes a fault. Note: Fault detection applies to both positive and negative inputs. For instance, if you specify a lower limit of 2 mA and an upper limit of 12 mA, NI-DAQmx detects a fault at 15 mA and -15 mA, but not at -6 mA because it is in the range of -12 mA to -2 mA.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | AI.InputLimitsFaultDetect.UpperLimit |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr318d.html language=enus -->

Note: Fault detection applies to both positive and negative inputs. For instance, if you specify a lower limit of 2 mA and an upper limit of 12 mA, NI-DAQmx detects a

### Analog Input:General Properties:Advanced:Input Limits Fault Detection:Lower Limit

Specifies the level of the lower limit for input limits detection. An input sample outside the upper and lower bounds causes a fault. Note: Fault detection applies to both positive and negative inputs. For instance, if you specify a lower limit of 2 mA and an upper limit of 12 mA, NI-DAQmx detects a fault at 15 mA and -15 mA, but not at -6 mA because it is in the range of -12 mA to -2 mA.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | AI.InputLimitsFaultDetect.LowerLimit |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

Parent topic:

### Counter Input:Frequency:Input:Hysteresis

Specifies a hysteresis level to apply to 
 [CI.Freq.ThreshVoltage](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr31ab)
 . When 
 [CI.Freq.StartingEdge](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr799)
 is rising, the source signal must first fall below 
 [CI.Freq.ThreshVoltage](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr31ab)
 minus the hysteresis before a rising edge is detected at 
 [CI.Freq.ThreshVoltage](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr31ab)
 . When 
 [CI.Freq.StartingEdge](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr799)
 is falling, the source signal must first rise above 
 [CI.Freq.ThreshVoltage](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr31ab)
 plus the hysteresis before a falling edge is detected at 
 [CI.Freq.ThreshVoltage](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr31ab)
 .

## TOPIC 01081: Counter Input:Count Edges:Gate:Input:Hysteresis

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31b6.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr31b6.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies a hysteresis level applied to the CI.CountEdges.Gate.ThreshVoltage . When CI.CountEdges.Gate.When is High, the source signal must fall below CI.CountEdges.Gate.ThreshVoltage minus the hysteresis before the counter resumes counting. When CI.CountEdges.Gate.When is Low, the source signal mus

### Counter Input:Count Edges:Gate:Input:Hysteresis

Specifies a hysteresis level applied to the 
 [CI.CountEdges.Gate.ThreshVoltage](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr31b5)
 . When 
 [CI.CountEdges.Gate.When](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr30f5)
 is High, the source signal must fall below 
 [CI.CountEdges.Gate.ThreshVoltage](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr31b5)
 minus the hysteresis before the counter resumes counting. When 
 [CI.CountEdges.Gate.When](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr30f5)
 is Low, the source signal must rise above 
 [CI.CountEdges.Gate.ThreshVoltage](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr31b5)
 plus the hysteresis before the counter resumes counting.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.CountEdges.Gate.Hyst |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

### Counter Output:General Properties:Counter Timebase:Source

Specifies the terminal of the timebase to use for the counter. Typically, NI-DAQmx uses one of the internal counter timebases when generating pulses. Use this property to specify an external timebase and produce custom pulse widths that are not possible using the internal timebases.

### Analog Input:General Properties:Digitizer/ADC:Dither:Enable

Specifies whether to enable dithering. Dithering adds Gaussian noise to the input signal. You can use dithering to achieve higher resolution measurements by over sampling the input signal and averaging the results.

| Frequency | 10181 | Frequency measurement using a frequency to voltage converter. |

| Force:Bridge | 15899 | Force measurement using a bridge-based sensor. |
| Force:IEPE Sensor | 15895 | Force measurement using an IEPE Sensor. |
| Pressure:Bridge | 15902 | Pressure measurement using a bridge-based sensor. |
| Sound Pressure:Microphone | 10354 | Sound pressure measurement using a microphone. |
| Torque:Bridge | 15905 | Torque measurement using a bridge-based sensor. |

## TOPIC 01131: Counter Input:Position:Z Index Phase

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr889.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-channel/attr889.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the states at which signal A and signal B must be while signal Z is high for NI-DAQmx to reset the measurement. If signal Z is never high while signal A and signal B are high, for example, you must choose a phase other than A High B High. When signal Z transitions to high and how long it s

### Counter Input:Position:Z Index Phase

Specifies the states at which signal A and signal B must be while signal Z is high for NI-DAQmx to reset the measurement. If signal Z is never high while signal A and signal B are high, for example, you must choose a phase other than A High B High.

When signal Z transitions to high and how long it stays high varies from encoder to encoder. Refer to the documentation for the encoder to determine the timing of signal Z with respect to signal A and signal B.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.Encoder.ZIndexPhase |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | True |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

| A High B High | 10040 | Reset the measurement when signal A and signal B are high. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| A High B Low | 10041 | Reset the measurement when signal A is high and signal B is low. |
| A Low B High | 10042 | Reset the measurement when signal A is low and signal B high. |
| A Low B Low | 10043 | Reset the measurement when signal A and signal B are low. |

Parent topic:

DAQmx Channel Properties

- source_description: Specifies the ratio of lateral strain to axial strain in the material you are measuring. Remarks The following table lists the characteristics of this property. Short Name AI.StrainGage.PoissonRatio Data type cdbl.png Permissions Read/Write Resettable True Settable While Task Is Running device-speci

### Analog Input:Strain:Strain Gage:Poisson Ratio

Specifies the ratio of lateral strain to axial strain in the material you are measuring.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | AI.StrainGage.PoissonRatio |
| --- | --- |

## TOPIC 01144: DAQmx Device Properties

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device-p.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device-p.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: The DAQmx Device properties return information about devices installed in your system.

### DAQmx Device Properties

The DAQmx Device properties return information about devices installed in your system.

- [Active Device](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr1854.html) Specifies the device from which to retrieve properties.
- [Bus:Number of DMA Channels](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr233c.html) Indicates the number of DMA channels on the device.
- [Chassis:Module Device Names](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr29b6.html) Indicates an array containing the names of the modules in the chassis.
- [Device Is Simulated](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr22ca.html) Indicates if the device is a simulated device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Bridge:Ranges](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2fd0.html) Indicates pairs of input voltage ratio ranges, in volts per volt, supported by devices that acquire using ratiometric measurements. Each pair consists of the low value followed by the high value.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Charge:Ranges](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3111.html) Indicates in coulombs pairs of input charge ranges for the device. Each pair consists of the low value followed by the high value.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Couplings](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2994.html) Indicates the coupling types supported by this device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Current:Internal Excitation:Discrete Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr29cb.html) Indicates the set of discrete internal current excitation values supported by this device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Current:Ranges](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2991.html) Indicates the pairs of current input ranges supported by this device. Each pair consists of the low value, followed by the high value.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Filter:Analog Low Pass:Cutoff Frequency:Discrete Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2995.html) Indicates the set of discrete lowpass cutoff frequencies supported by this device. If the device supports ranges of lowpass cutoff frequencies, use AI.Lowpass.CutoffFreq.RangeVals to determine supported frequencies.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Filter:Analog Low Pass:Cutoff Frequency:Range Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr29cf.html) Indicates pairs of lowpass cutoff frequency ranges supported by this device. Each pair consists of the low value, followed by the high value. If the device supports a set of discrete lowpass cutoff frequencies, use AI.Lowpass.CutoffFreq.DiscreteVals to determine the supported frequencies.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Filter:Digital Filter:Low Pass:Cutoff Frequency:Discrete Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr30c8.html) Indicates the set of discrete lowpass cutoff frequencies supported by this device. If the device supports ranges of lowpass cutoff frequencies, use AI.DigFltr.Lowpass.CutoffFreq.RangeVals to determine supported frequencies.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Filter:Digital Filter:Low Pass:Cutoff Frequency:Range Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr30c9.html) Indicates pairs of lowpass cutoff frequency ranges supported by this device. Each pair consists of the low value, followed by the high value. If the device supports a set of discrete lowpass cutoff frequencies, use AI.DigFltr.Lowpass.CutoffFreq.DiscreteVals to determine the supported frequencies.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Filter:Digital Filter:Types](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3107.html) Indicates the AI digital filter types supported by the device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Frequency:Ranges](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2992.html) Indicates the pairs of frequency input ranges supported by this device. Each pair consists of the low value, followed by the high value.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Gains](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2993.html) Indicates the input gain settings supported by this device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Measurement Types](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2fd2.html) Indicates the measurement types supported by the physical channels of the device. Refer to AI.MeasTypes for information on specific channels.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Physical Channels](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr231e.html) Indicates an array containing the names of the analog input physical channels available on the device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Resistance:Ranges](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2a15.html) Indicates pairs of input resistance ranges, in ohms, supported by devices that have the necessary signal conditioning to measure resistances. Each pair consists of the low value followed by the high value.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Timing:Maximum Multiple Channel Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr298d.html) Indicates the maximum sampling rate for an analog input task from this device. To find the maximum rate for the task, take the minimum of AI.MaxSingleChanRate or the indicated sampling rate of this device divided by the number of channels to acquire data from (including cold-junction compensation and autozero channels).
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Timing:Maximum Single Channel Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr298c.html) Indicates the maximum rate for an analog input task if the task contains only a single channel from this device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Timing:Minimum Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr298e.html) Indicates the minimum rate for an analog input task on this device. NI-DAQmx returns a warning or error if you attempt to sample at a slower rate.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Timing:Number of Sample Timing Engines](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3163.html) Indicates the number of Analog Input sample timing engines supported by the device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Timing:Number of Synchronization Pulse Sources](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3164.html) Indicates the number of Analog Input synchronization pulse sources supported by the device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Timing:Sample Modes](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2fdc.html) Indicates sample modes supported by devices that support sample clocked analog input.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Timing:Simultaneous Sampling Supported](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr298f.html) Indicates if the device supports simultaneous sampling.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Trigger:Trigger Usage](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2986.html) Indicates the triggers supported by this device for an analog input task.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Voltage:Internal Excitation:Discrete Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr29c9.html) Indicates the set of discrete internal voltage excitation values supported by this device. If the device supports ranges of internal excitation values, use AI.Voltage.IntExcit.RangeVals to determine supported excitation values.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Voltage:Internal Excitation:Range Values](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr29ca.html) Indicates pairs of internal voltage excitation ranges supported by this device. Each pair consists of the low value, followed by the high value. If the device supports a set of discrete internal excitation values, use AI.Voltage.IntExcit.DiscreteVals to determine the supported excitation values.
- [I/O Type:Analog Input:Voltage:Ranges](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2990.html) Indicates pairs of input voltage ranges supported by this device. Each pair consists of the low value, followed by the high value.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Current:Ranges](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr299c.html) Indicates pairs of output current ranges supported by this device. Each pair consists of the low value, followed by the high value.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Gains](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr299d.html) Indicates the output gain settings supported by this device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Output Types](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2fd3.html) Indicates the generation types supported by the physical channels of the device. Refer to AO.OutputTypes for information on specific channels.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Physical Channels](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr231f.html) Indicates an array containing the names of the analog output physical channels available on the device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Timing:Maximum Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2997.html) Indicates the maximum analog output rate of the device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Timing:Minimum Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2998.html) Indicates the minimum analog output rate of the device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Timing:Number of Sample Timing Engines](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3165.html) Indicates the number of Analog Output sample timing engines supported by the device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Timing:Number of Synchronization Pulse Sources](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3166.html) Indicates the number of Analog Output synchronization pulse sources supported by the device.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Timing:Sample Clock Supported](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2996.html) Indicates if the device supports the sample clock timing type for analog output tasks.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Timing:Sample Modes](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2fdd.html) Indicates sample modes supported by devices that support sample clocked analog output.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Trigger:Trigger Usage](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2987.html) Indicates the triggers supported by this device for analog output tasks.
- [I/O Type:Analog Output:Voltage:Ranges](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr299b.html) Indicates pairs of output voltage ranges supported by this device. Each pair consists of the low value, followed by the high value.
- [I/O Type:Counter Input:Maximum Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr299f.html) Indicates in bits the size of the counters on the device.
- [I/O Type:Counter Input:Maximum Timebase](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr29a0.html) Indicates in hertz the maximum counter timebase frequency.
- [I/O Type:Counter Input:Measurement Types](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2fd4.html) Indicates the measurement types supported by the physical channels of the device. Refer to CI.MeasTypes for information on specific channels.
- [I/O Type:Counter Input:Physical Channels](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2324.html) Indicates an array containing the names of the counter input physical channels available on the device.
- [I/O Type:Counter Input:Timing:Sample Clock Supported](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr299e.html) Indicates if the device supports the sample clock timing type for counter input tasks.
- [I/O Type:Counter Input:Timing:Sample Modes](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2fde.html) Indicates sample modes supported by devices that support sample clocked counter input.
- [I/O Type:Counter Input:Trigger:Trigger Usage](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr298a.html) Indicates the triggers supported by this device for counter input tasks.
- [I/O Type:Counter Output:Maximum Size](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr29a1.html) Indicates in bits the size of the counters on the device.
- [I/O Type:Counter Output:Maximum Timebase](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr29a2.html) Indicates in hertz the maximum counter timebase frequency.
- [I/O Type:Counter Output:Output Types](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2fd5.html) Indicates the generation types supported by the physical channels of the device. Refer to CO.OutputTypes for information on specific channels.
- [I/O Type:Counter Output:Physical Channels](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2325.html) Indicates an array containing the names of the counter output physical channels available on the device.
- [I/O Type:Counter Output:Timing:Sample Clock Supported](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2f5b.html) Indicates if the device supports Sample Clock timing for counter output tasks.
- [I/O Type:Counter Output:Timing:SampleModes](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2fdf.html) Indicates sample modes supported by devices that support sample clocked counter output.
- [I/O Type:Counter Output:Trigger:Trigger Usage](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr298b.html) Indicates the triggers supported by this device for counter output tasks.
- [I/O Type:Digital Input:Lines](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2320.html) Indicates an array containing the names of the digital input lines available on the device.
- [I/O Type:Digital Input:Ports](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2321.html) Indicates an array containing the names of the digital input ports available on the device.
- [I/O Type:Digital Input:Timing:Maximum Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2999.html) Indicates the maximum digital input rate of the device.
- [I/O Type:Digital Input:Timing:Number of Sample Timing Engines](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3167.html) Indicates the number of Digital Input sample timing engines supported by the device.
- [I/O Type:Digital Input:Trigger:Trigger Usage](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2988.html) Indicates the triggers supported by this device for digital input tasks.
- [I/O Type:Digital Output:Lines](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2322.html) Indicates an array containing the names of the digital output lines available on the device.
- [I/O Type:Digital Output:Ports](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2323.html) Indicates an array containing the names of the digital output ports available on the device.
- [I/O Type:Digital Output:Timing:Maximum Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr299a.html) Indicates the maximum digital output rate of the device.
- [I/O Type:Digital Output:Timing:Number of Sample Timing Engines](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3168.html) Indicates the number of Digital Output synchronization pulse sources supported by the device.
- [I/O Type:Digital Output:Trigger:Trigger Usage](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2989.html) Indicates the triggers supported by this device for digital output tasks.
- [Identification:Accessory:Product Numbers](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2f6e.html) Indicates the unique hardware identification number for accessories connected to the device. Each array element corresponds to a connector. For example, index 0 corresponds to connector 0. The array contains 0 for each connector with no accessory connected.
- [Identification:Accessory:Product Types](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2f6d.html) Indicates the model names of accessories connected to the device. Each array element corresponds to a connector. For example, index 0 corresponds to connector 0. The array contains an empty string for each connector with no accessory connected.
- [Identification:Accessory:Serial Numbers](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2f6f.html) Indicates the serial number for accessories connected to the device. Each array element corresponds to a connector. For example, index 0 corresponds to connector 0. The array contains 0 for each connector with no accessory connected.
- [Identification:Carrier Serial Number](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2a8a.html) Indicates the serial number of the device carrier. This value is zero if the carrier does not have a serial number.
- [Identification:Device Serial Number](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr632.html) Indicates the serial number of the device. This value is zero if the device does not have a serial number.
- [Identification:FieldDAQ:Bank Device Names](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3178.html) Indicates an array containing the names of the banks in the FieldDAQ.
- [Identification:FieldDAQ:Device Name](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3171.html) Indicates the parent device which this bank is located in.
- [Identification:ID Pin:Memory Family Codes](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr31f3.html) Indicates the family code of the memory connected to each ID Pin. Each array element corresponds to an ID Pin. The array contains 0 for each ID Pin with no memory connected.
- [Identification:ID Pin:Memory Serial Numbers](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr31f4.html) Indicates the serial number of the memory connected to each ID Pin. Each array element corresponds to an ID Pin. The array contains an empty string for each ID Pin with no memory connected.
- [Identification:ID Pin:Memory Sizes](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr31f5.html) Indicates the size in bytes of the memory connected to each ID Pin. Each array element corresponds to an ID Pin. The array contains 0 for each ID Pin with no memory connected.
- [Identification:ID Pin:Pin Names](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr31f1.html) Indicates the names of all the ID Pins on this device.
- [Identification:ID Pin:Pin Statuses](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr31f2.html) Indicates status of each ID Pin.
- [Identification:Product Category](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr29a9.html) Indicates the product category of the device. This category corresponds to the category displayed in MAX when creating NI-DAQmx simulated devices.
- [Identification:Product Number](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr231d.html) Indicates the unique hardware identification number for the device.
- [Identification:Product Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr631.html) Indicates the product name of the device.
- [Location:Bus Type](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2326.html) Indicates the bus type of the device.
- [Location:CompactDAQ:Chassis Device Name](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr29b7.html) Indicates the name of the CompactDAQ chassis that contains this module.
- [Location:CompactDAQ:Slot Number](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr29b8.html) Indicates the slot number in which this module is located in the CompactDAQ chassis.
- [Location:CompactRIO:Chassis Device Name](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3161.html) Indicates the name of the CompactRIO chassis that contains this module.
- [Location:CompactRIO:Slot Number](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3162.html) Indicates the slot number of the CompactRIO chassis where this module is located.
- [Location:PCI:Bus Number](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2327.html) Indicates the PCI bus number of the device.
- [Location:PCI:Device Number](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2328.html) Indicates the PCI slot number of the device.
- [Location:PXI:Chassis Number](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2329.html) Indicates the PXI chassis number of the device, as identified in MAX.
- [Location:PXI:Slot Number](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr232a.html) Indicates the PXI slot number of the device.
- [Location:TCP/IP:Ethernet IP Address](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2a8c.html) Indicates the IPv4 address of the Ethernet interface in dotted decimal format. This property returns 0.0.0.0 if the Ethernet interface cannot acquire an address.
- [Location:TCP/IP:Hostname](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2a8b.html) Indicates the IPv4 hostname of the device.
- [Location:TCP/IP:Wireless IP Address](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2a8d.html) Indicates the IPv4 address of the 802.11 wireless interface in dotted decimal format. This property returns 0.0.0.0 if the wireless interface cannot acquire an address.
- [TEDS:Hardware TEDS Supported](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2fd6.html) Indicates whether the device supports hardware TEDS.
- [Terminals](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2a40.html) Indicates a list of all terminals on the device.
- [Time:Number of Time Triggers](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3141.html) Indicates the number of time triggers available on the device.
- [Time:Number of Timestamp Engines](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr3142.html) Indicates the number of timestamp engines available on the device.
- [Triggering:Analog Triggering Supported](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2984.html) Indicates if the device supports analog triggering.
- [Triggering:Digital Triggering Supported](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr2985.html) Indicates if the device supports digital triggering.
- [Triggering:Time Triggering Supported](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-device/attr301f.html) Indicates whether the device supports time triggering.

## TOPIC 01147: Identification:Product Number

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`

### Identification:Product Number

Indicates the unique 
 [hardware identification number](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxdevconsid_hardwareids)
 for the device.

#### Remarks

### I/O Type:Analog Input:Timing:Maximum Multiple Channel Rate

Indicates the maximum sampling rate for an analog input task from this device. To find the maximum rate for the task, take the minimum of 
 [AI.MaxSingleChanRate](/csh?context=nidaqmx_daqmxprop_attr298c)
 or the indicated sampling rate of this device divided by the number of channels to acquire data from (including cold-junction compensation and autozero channels).

| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read Only |
| Resettable | False |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

### I/O Type:Counter Input:Measurement Types

 for information on specific channels.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | CI.MeasTypes |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read Only |
| Resettable | False |
| Settable While Task Is Running | device-specific |
| Available in Run-Time Engine | True |

| Count Edges | 10125 | Count edges of a digital signal. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Frequency | 10179 | Measure the frequency of a digital signal. |
| Period | 10256 | Measure the period of a digital signal. |
| Pulse Width | 10359 | Measure the width of a pulse of a digital signal. |
| Semi Period | 10289 | Measure the time between state transitions of a digital signal. |
| Pulse Frequency | 15864 | Pulse measurement, returning the result as frequency and duty cycle. |
| Pulse Time | 15865 | Pulse measurement, returning the result as high time and low time. |
| Pulse Ticks | 15866 | Pulse measurement, returning the result as high ticks and low ticks. |
| Duty Cycle | 16070 | Measure the duty cycle of a digital signal. |
| Position:Angular Encoder | 10360 | Angular position measurement using an angular encoder. |
| Position:Linear Encoder | 10361 | Linear position measurement using a linear encoder. |
| Velocity:Angular Encoder | 16078 | Angular velocity measurement using an angular encoder. |
| Velocity:Linear Encoder | 16079 | Linear velocity measurement using a linear encoder. |
| Two Edge Separation | 10267 | Measure time between edges of two digital signals. |
| GPS Timestamp | 10362 | Timestamp measurement, synchronizing the counter to a GPS receiver. |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal-p.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 01245: DAQmx Export Signal Properties

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal-p.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal-p.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the DAQmx Export Signal properties to route a control signal within a device or from one device to another. These routes are task-based and are useful for sharing clocks and triggers among multiple devices.

### DAQmx Export Signal Properties

Use the DAQmx Export Signal properties to route a control signal within a device or from one device to another. These routes are task-based and are useful for sharing clocks and triggers among multiple devices.

- [Clocks:10MHz Reference Clock:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr226e.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the 10MHz Clock.
- [Clocks:20MHz Timebase:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1657.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the 20MHz Timebase.
- [Clocks:AI Convert Clock:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1687.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the AI Convert Clock.
- [Clocks:AI Convert Clock:Pulse:Polarity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1688.html) Indicates the polarity of the exported AI Convert Clock. The polarity is fixed and independent of the active edge of the source of the AI Convert Clock.
- [Clocks:Divided Sample Clock Timebase:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr21a1.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Divided Sample Clock Timebase.
- [Clocks:Sample Clock Timebase:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr18f9.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Sample Clock Timebase.
- [Clocks:Sample Clock:Delay Offset](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr21c4.html) Specifies in seconds the amount of time to offset the exported Sample clock. Refer to timing diagrams for generation applications in the device documentation for more information about this value.
- [Clocks:Sample Clock:Output Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr186b.html) Specifies whether the exported Sample Clock issues a pulse at the beginning of a sample or changes to a high state for the duration of the sample.
- [Clocks:Sample Clock:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1663.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Sample Clock.
- [Clocks:Sample Clock:Pulse:Polarity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1664.html) Specifies the polarity of the exported Sample Clock if SampClk.OutputBehavior is Pulse.
- [Events:AI Hold Complete Event:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr18ed.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the AI Hold Complete Event.
- [Events:AI Hold Complete Event:Pulse:Polarity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr18ee.html) Specifies the polarity of an exported AI Hold Complete Event pulse.
- [Events:Advance Complete Event:Delay Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1757.html) Specifies the output signal delay in periods of the sample clock.
- [Events:Advance Complete Event:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1651.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Advance Complete Event.
- [Events:Advance Complete Event:Pulse:Polarity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1652.html) Specifies the polarity of the exported Advance Complete Event.
- [Events:Advance Complete Event:Pulse:Width Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1654.html) Specifies the width of the exported Advance Complete Event pulse.
- [Events:Change Detection Event:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr2197.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Change Detection Event.
- [Events:Change Detection Event:Pulse:Polarity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr2303.html) Specifies the polarity of an exported Change Detection Event pulse.
- [Events:Counter Output Event:Output Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr174f.html) Specifies whether the exported Counter Output Event pulses or changes from one state to the other when the counter reaches terminal count.
- [Events:Counter Output Event:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1717.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Counter Output Event.
- [Events:Counter Output Event:Pulse:Polarity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1718.html) Specifies the polarity of the pulses at the output terminal of the counter when CtrOutEvent.OutputBehavior is Pulse. NI-DAQmx ignores this property if CtrOutEvent.OutputBehavior is Toggle.
- [Events:Counter Output Event:Toggle:Idle State](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr186a.html) Specifies the initial state of the output terminal of the counter when CtrOutEvent.OutputBehavior is Toggle. The terminal enters this state when NI-DAQmx commits the task.
- [Events:Data Active Event:Level:Active Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1634.html) Specifies the polarity of the exported Data Active Event.
- [Events:Data Active Event:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1633.html) Specifies the terminal to which to export the Data Active Event.
- [Events:Handshake Event:Delay Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr22bc.html) Specifies the number of seconds to delay after the Handshake Trigger deasserts before asserting the Handshake Event.
- [Events:Handshake Event:Interlocked:Assert on Start](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr22be.html) Specifies to assert the Handshake Event when the task starts if HshkEvent.OutputBehavior is Interlocked.
- [Events:Handshake Event:Interlocked:Asserted Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr22bd.html) Specifies the asserted level of the exported Handshake Event if HshkEvent.OutputBehavior is Interlocked.
- [Events:Handshake Event:Interlocked:Deassert Delay Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr22bf.html) Specifies in seconds the amount of time to wait after the Handshake Trigger asserts before deasserting the Handshake Event if HshkEvent.OutputBehavior is Interlocked.
- [Events:Handshake Event:Output Behavior](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr22bb.html) Specifies the output behavior of the Handshake Event.
- [Events:Handshake Event:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr22ba.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Handshake Event.
- [Events:Handshake Event:Pulse:Polarity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr22c0.html) Specifies the polarity of the exported Handshake Event if HshkEvent.OutputBehavior is Pulse.
- [Events:Handshake Event:Pulse:Width Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr22c1.html) Specifies in seconds the pulse width of the exported Handshake Event if HshkEvent.OutputBehavior is Pulse.
- [Events:Ready For Start Event:Level:Active Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1751.html) Specifies the polarity of the exported Ready for Start Event.
- [Events:Ready For Start Event:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1609.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Ready for Start Event.
- [Events:Ready For Transfer Event:Deassert Condition](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr2963.html) Specifies when the ready for transfer event deasserts.
- [Events:Ready For Transfer Event:Deassert Condition Custom Threshold](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr2964.html) Specifies in samples the threshold below which the Ready for Transfer Event deasserts. This threshold is an amount of space available in the onboard memory of the device. RdyForXferEvent.DeassertCond must be Onboard Memory Custom Threshold to use a custom threshold.
- [Events:Ready For Transfer Event:Level:Active Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr22b6.html) Specifies the active level of the exported Ready for Transfer Event.
- [Events:Ready For Transfer Event:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr22b5.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Ready for Transfer Event.
- [Events:Synchronization Pulse Event:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr223c.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Synchronization Pulse Event.
- [Events:Watchdog Timer Expired Event:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr21aa.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Watchdog Timer Expired Event.
- [Triggers:Advance Trigger:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1645.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Advance Trigger.
- [Triggers:Advance Trigger:Pulse:Polarity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1646.html) Indicates the polarity of the exported Advance Trigger.
- [Triggers:Advance Trigger:Pulse:Width Units](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1647.html) Specifies the units of AdvTrig.Pulse.Width .
- [Triggers:Advance Trigger:Pulse:Width Value](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1648.html) Specifies the width of an exported Advance Trigger pulse. Specify this value in the units you specify with AdvTrig.Pulse.WidthUnits .
- [Triggers:Pause Trigger:Level:Active Level](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1616.html) Specifies the active level of the exported Pause Trigger.
- [Triggers:Pause Trigger:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr1615.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Pause Trigger.
- [Triggers:Reference Trigger:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr590.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Reference Trigger.
- [Triggers:Reference Trigger:Pulse:Polarity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr591.html) Specifies the polarity of the exported Reference Trigger.
- [Triggers:Start Trigger:Output Terminal](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr584.html) Specifies the terminal to which to route the Start Trigger.
- [Triggers:Start Trigger:Pulse:Polarity](../../../resource/objmgr/daqmx-rc/daqmx-export-signal/attr585.html) Specifies the polarity of the exported Start Trigger.
